This charming studio is located in one of the best, most central and safest locations in LA - Beverly Hills. It is bright, and located on the second floor of a quaint 2 story building. The studio has hardwood floors, is fully furnished (modern) and includes all of the amenities - a toaster oven, and a microwave plus I will provide a cleaning person every 3 weeks! The apartment is in one of the most posh neighborhoods in Los Angeles - Beverly Hills and right in the center of Beverly Hills (on Wilshire) next to Saks Fifth Avenue, 2 minutes from Barneys, Neiman Marcus, etc. Its a five minute walk to Rodeo Drive and world famous restaurants and hotels such as: Mr. Chows, Maestros, the Beverly Regent and the Cut, the Montage and Bouchon, as well as all the shops and restaurants on South Beverly Drive...Landmarks such as the Beverly Regent and Rodeo Collection are a 2 minute walk from the apartment. The hippest shopping areas in LA - Robertson and 3rd street are a 5 minute drive. In 15 minutes you're at the BEACH and in 10 minutes you're in West Hollywood and Hollywood partying at the trendiest bars and clubs. The apartment is in a security building and includes: Apple TV, wifi, a heater and AC, an underground parking space as well as a parking permit, and laundry on the premises. There is a separate hallway with a connecting bathroom and a walk-in closet. The kitchen is a separate room and has a dining table, a microwave and toaster oven. I can rent my fabulous studio for 3 months or for longer. It is ideal for a people who want to live in an extremely safe neighborhood, like to walk and live literally within 5 minutes from the gym, restaurants, coffee bars, juice bars, department stores, etc... There are buses right on Wilshire, which take you to all different parts of Los Angeles. Beverly Hills is close to West Hollywood, Culver City, Westwood and UCLA, and Santa Monica. I cherish my home and am looking for a responsible person to treat it with respect. If you would like a monthly rental term - this is available for $3200 per month or $6200 for 2 months I look forward to hearing from you!

There's a brand new 51" Plasma HDTV smart TV and blue 3D player in the living room. Weekly house cleaning and gardening will also be provided. . There are 3 bedrooms and 3 baths Including a full, private master suite. There are 2 full bathrooms upstairs and a third bathroom on the first floor that has a stall shower. Two of the three bedrooms have balconies overlooking lush trees in the large back yard. The first floor has a custom slate floor, a wood burning / gas fireplace and a wet bar. There's a laundry room in this apartment with a large capacity washer &amp; dryer. The kitchen is fully equipped with a stove, oven, microwave, dishwasher, large refrigerator, etc. There's a kitchenette that seats 6 and also a separate dining room. Carport parking for 3 cars is provided. The large back yard (15’ x 50’) provides charming shaded areas for dining and leisure and is exclusively for your use. The apartment sleeps 6 easily but can accommodate more. All sheets, blankets, towels, pots and pans, dishes, silverware, etc., are provided at no charge. There are buses close by that take you quickly to Santa Monica, downtown Los Angeles, Hollywood, etc. This neighborhood is very safe and convenient to everything.
